# Non-Dual Equations

The following equations have no dual to any other.

* Equation1[(x = x)]
* Equation2[(x = y)]
* Equation3[(x = (x ◇ x))]
* Equation6[(x = (y ◇ y))]
* Equation7[(x = (y ◇ z))]
* Equation40[((x ◇ x) = (y ◇ y))]
* Equation41[((x ◇ x) = (y ◇ z))]
* Equation43[((x ◇ y) = (y ◇ x))]
* Equation44[((x ◇ y) = (y ◇ z))]
* Equation46[((x ◇ y) = (z ◇ w))]
* Equation151[(x = ((x ◇ x) ◇ (x ◇ x)))]
* Equation159[(x = ((x ◇ y) ◇ (y ◇ x)))]
* Equation162[(x = ((x ◇ y) ◇ (z ◇ x)))]
* Equation167[(x = ((y ◇ x) ◇ (x ◇ y)))]
* Equation168[(x = ((y ◇ x) ◇ (x ◇ z)))]
* Equation180[(x = ((y ◇ y) ◇ (y ◇ y)))]
* Equation184[(x = ((y ◇ y) ◇ (z ◇ z)))]
* Equation192[(x = ((y ◇ z) ◇ (y ◇ z)))]
* Equation195[(x = ((y ◇ z) ◇ (z ◇ y)))]
* Equation197[(x = ((y ◇ z) ◇ (z ◇ w)))]
* Equation199[(x = ((y ◇ z) ◇ (w ◇ y)))]
* Equation202[(x = ((y ◇ z) ◇ (w ◇ u)))]
* Equation3659[((x ◇ x) = ((x ◇ x) ◇ (x ◇ x)))]
* Equation3667[((x ◇ x) = ((x ◇ y) ◇ (y ◇ x)))]
* Equation3670[((x ◇ x) = ((x ◇ y) ◇ (z ◇ x)))]
* Equation3675[((x ◇ x) = ((y ◇ x) ◇ (x ◇ y)))]
* Equation3676[((x ◇ x) = ((y ◇ x) ◇ (x ◇ z)))]
* Equation3688[((x ◇ x) = ((y ◇ y) ◇ (y ◇ y)))]
* Equation3692[((x ◇ x) = ((y ◇ y) ◇ (z ◇ z)))]
* Equation3700[((x ◇ x) = ((y ◇ z) ◇ (y ◇ z)))]
* Equation3703[((x ◇ x) = ((y ◇ z) ◇ (z ◇ y)))]
* Equation3705[((x ◇ x) = ((y ◇ z) ◇ (z ◇ w)))]
* Equation3707[((x ◇ x) = ((y ◇ z) ◇ (w ◇ y)))]
* Equation3710[((x ◇ x) = ((y ◇ z) ◇ (w ◇ u)))]
* Equation3715[((x ◇ y) = ((x ◇ x) ◇ (y ◇ y)))]
* Equation3722[((x ◇ y) = ((x ◇ y) ◇ (x ◇ y)))]
* Equation3740[((x ◇ y) = ((x ◇ z) ◇ (z ◇ y)))]
* Equation3744[((x ◇ y) = ((x ◇ z) ◇ (w ◇ y)))]
* Equation3751[((x ◇ y) = ((y ◇ x) ◇ (y ◇ x)))]
* Equation3758[((x ◇ y) = ((y ◇ y) ◇ (x ◇ x)))]
* Equation3776[((x ◇ y) = ((y ◇ z) ◇ (z ◇ x)))]
